\hypertarget{group__Display}{}\doxysection{Display}
\label{group__Display}\index{Display@{Display}}


functions and variables for the display are mainly for the visual monitoring but could also be part of certain processing routines, The file is based on\+: \href{https://github.com/soonuse/epd-library-stm32/tree/master/1.54inch_e-paper}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/soonuse/epd-\/library-\/stm32/tree/master/1.\+54inch\+\_\+e-\/paper}}

\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
functions and variables for the display are mainly for the visual monitoring but could also be part of certain processing routines, The file is based on\+: \href{https://github.com/soonuse/epd-library-stm32/tree/master/1.54inch_e-paper}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/soonuse/epd-\/library-\/stm32/tree/master/1.\+54inch\+\_\+e-\/paper}}
